25/* The following table can be generated from the file
26 unix/mappings/eastasia/jis/shiftjis.txt
27 from the Unicode CD (also available on their FTP server) using
28 the command
29
30 egrep '^0x8[01234][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
31 /mnt/cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/jis/shiftjis.txt | perl ~/sjis.pl
32
33 where sjis.pl contains:
34
35 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
36 while (<>) {
37 local($sjis, $ucs, %rest) = split;
38 $sjis = hex($sjis) - 0x8140;
39 local($sidx) = int($sjis / 256) * 192 + ($sjis % 256);
40 printf "\n " if (($n % 4) == 0);
41 ++$n;
42 printf " [%4d] = %s,", $sidx, $ucs;
43 }
44 print "\n";
45 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
46*/
47

194 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

197 $sjis = hex($sjis) - 0x8840;

1857/* The following table can be generated using
1858
1859 awk '/^0x/ { print $2, $1; }' < .../eastasia/jis/shiftjis.txt |
1860 egrep "^0x00[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]" |
1861 sort -u | perl tab.pl
1862
1863 where tab.pl is
1864
1865 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1866 $n=0;
1867 while (<>) {
1868 local($ucs4, $sjis, %rest) = split;
1869 local($u)=hex($ucs4);
1870 local($s)=hex($sjis);
1871 printf ("\n ") if ($n % 3 == 0);
1872 ++$n;
1873 printf (" [0x%04x] = \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",", $u,
1874 $s < 0x100 ? $s : int($s/256), $s < 0x100 ? 0 : $s&255);
1875 }
1876 printf ("\n");
1877 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1878
1879 The only problem is that the shiftjis.txt file does not contain the
1880 mapping for the characters 0x00 to 0x1f. We add them ourself.
1881
1882 A much bigger problem is that mapping of the tilde and the backslash
1883 character. There are no such characters in SJIS. The proposed
1884 handling is to simply map the two input values to the corresponding
1885 byte values of ASCII. Things fall more or less in place this way.
1886*/
1887static const char from_ucs4_lat1[0xf8][2] =
1888{

4313
4314/* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function. */
4315#define CHARSET_NAME "SJIS//"
4316#define FROM_LOOP from_sjis
4317#define TO_LOOP to_sjis
4318#define DEFINE_INIT 1
4319#define DEFINE_FINI 1
4320#define MIN_NEEDED_FROM 1
4321#define MAX_NEEDED_FROM 2
4322#define MIN_NEEDED_TO 4
4323#define ONE_DIRECTION 0
4324
4325/* First define the conversion function from SJIS to UCS4. */
4326#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4327#define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4328#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4329#define LOOPFCT FROM_LOOP
4330#define BODY \
4331 { \
4332 uint32_t ch = *inptr; \
4333 \
4334 if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0x5c) \
4335 { \
4336 ch = 0xa5; \
4337 ++inptr; \
4338 } \
4339 else if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0x7e) \
4340 { \
4341 ch = 0x203e; \
4342 ++inptr; \
4343 } \
4344 else if (ch < 0x80) \
4345 ++inptr; \
4346 else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xdf) \
4347 { \
4348 ch += 0xfec0; \
4349 ++inptr; \
4350 } \
4351 else if (__builtin_expect (ch > 0xea, 0) \
4352 || __builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0xa0 \
4353 || __builtin_expect (ch <= 0x80, 0)) \
4354 { \
4355 /* These are illegal. */ \
4356 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
4357 } \
4358 else \
4359 { \
4360 /* Two-byte character. First test whether the next byte \
4361 is also available. */ \
4362 uint32_t ch2; \
4363 uint_fast32_t idx; \
4364 \
4365 if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend)) \
4366 { \
4367 /* The second byte is not available. Store \
4368 the intermediate result. */ \
4369 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
4370 break; \
4371 } \
4372 \
4373 ch2 = inptr[1]; \
4374 idx = ch * 256 + ch2; \
4375 if (__glibc_unlikely (ch2 < 0x40)) \
4376 { \
4377 /* This is illegal. */ \
4378 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
4379 } \
4380 else if ((__builtin_expect (idx > 0x84be && idx < 0x889f, 0)) \
4381 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x88fc && idx < 0x8940, 0)) \
4382 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x9ffc && idx < 0xe040, 0)) \
4383 || __builtin_expect (idx > 0xeaa4, 0)) \
4384 { \
4385 /* This is illegal. */ \
4386 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2); \
4387 } \
4388 else \
4389 { \
4390 /* We could pack the data a bit more dense. The second \
4391 byte will never be 0x7f and it will also be never \
4392 >0xfc. But this would mean yet more `if's. */ \
4393 if (idx <= 0x84be) \
4394 ch = cjk_block1[(ch - 0x81) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4395 else if (idx <= 0x88fc) \
4396 ch = cjk_block2[(ch - 0x88) * 192 + ch2 - 0x9f]; \
4397 else if (idx <= 0x9ffc) \
4398 ch = cjk_block3[(ch - 0x89) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4399 else \
4400 ch = cjk_block4[(ch - 0xe0) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4401 \
4402 if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == 0)) \
4403 { \
4404 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4405 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2); \
4406 } \
4407 \
4408 inptr += 2; \
4409 } \
4410 } \
4411 \
4412 put32 (outptr, ch); \
4413 outptr += 4; \
4414 }
4415#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4416#define ONEBYTE_BODY \
4417 { \
4418 if (c < 0x80) \
4419 { \
4420 if (c == 0x5c) \
4421 return 0xa5; \
4422 if (c == 0x7e) \
4423 return 0x203e; \
4424 return c; \
4425 } \
4426 if (c >= 0xa1 && c <= 0xdf) \
4427 return 0xfec0 + c; \
4428 return WEOF; \
4429 }
4430#include <iconv/loop.c>
4431
4432
4433/* Next, define the other direction. */
4434#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4435#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4436#define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4437#define LOOPFCT TO_LOOP
4438#define BODY \
4439 { \
4440 uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr); \
4441 const char *cp; \
4442 \
4443 if (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1) / sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1[0]))) \
4444 { \
4445 if (ch >= 0x0391 && ch <= 0x0451) \
4446 cp = from_ucs4_greek[ch - 0x391]; \
4447 else if (ch >= 0x2010 && ch <= 0x9fa0) \
4448 cp = from_ucs4_cjk[ch - 0x02010]; \
4449 else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xff01, 1) \
4450 && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xffef, 1)) \
4451 cp = from_ucs4_extra[ch - 0xff00]; \
4452 else \
4453 { \
4454 UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4); \
4455 /* Illegal character. */ \
4456 cp = ""; \
4457 } \
4458 } \
4459 else \
4460 cp = from_ucs4_lat1[ch]; \
4461 \
4462 if (__builtin_expect (cp[0] == '\0', 0) && ch != 0) \
4463 { \
4464 /* Illegal character. */ \
4465 STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4); \
4466 } \
4467 else \
4468 { \
4469 *outptr = cp[0]; \
4470 /* Now test for a possible second byte and write this if possible. */\
4471 if (cp[1] != '\0') \
4472 { \
4473 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend)) \
4474 { \
4475 /* The result does not fit into the buffer. */ \
4476 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4477 break; \
4478 } \
4479 *++outptr = cp[1]; \
4480 } \
4481 ++outptr; \
4482 } \
4483 \
4484 inptr += 4; \
4485 }
4486#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4487#include <iconv/loop.c>
